Runtime\n        class MurphyRuntime {\n            constructor() {\n                this.terminalOutput = document.getElementById(\'terminalOutput\');\n                this.terminalInput = document.getElementById(\'terminalInput\');\n                this.operationCount = 0;\n                this.artifactCount = 0;\n                this.systemConfidence = 0.95;\n                this.setupEventListeners();\n            }\n\n            setupEventListeners() {\n                this.terminalInput.addEventListener(\'keypress\', (e) => {\n                    if (e.key === \'Enter\') {\n                        this.processInput(this.terminalInput.value);\n                        this.terminalInput.value = \'\';\n                    }\n                });\n\n                document.getElementById(\'approveBtn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n                    this.handleApproval(true);\n                });\n\n                document.getElementById(\'rejectBtn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n                    this.handleApproval(false);\n                });\n            }\n\n            addOutput(tag, message, confidence) {\n                const line = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                line.className = \'output-line\';\n                \n                const tagSpan = document.createElement(\'span\');\n                tagSpan.className = `tag-${tag.toLowerCase()}`;\n                tagSpan.textContent = `[${tag}]`;\n                \n                const          confBadge.className = `confidence-badge ${this.getConfidenceClass(confidence)}`;\n                confBadge.textContent = confidence.toFixed(2);\n                \n                line.appendChild(tagSpan);\n                line.appendChild(messageSpan);\n                line.appendChild(confBadge);\n                \n                this.terminalOutput.appendChild(line);\n                this.terminalOutput.scrollTop = this.terminalOutput.scrollHeight;\n            }\n\n            getConfidenceClass(conf) {\n                if (conf >= 0.8) return \'conf-high\';\n                if (conf >= 0.5) return \'conf-medium\';\n                return \'conf-low\';\n            }\n\n            updateMetrics() {\n                this.operationCount++;\n                document.getElementById(\'operationCount\').textContent = this.operationCount;\n                document.getElementById(\'systemConfidence\').textContent = this.systemConfidence.toFixed(2);\n                document.getElementById(\'confidenceBar\').style.width = (this.systemConfidence * 100) + \'%\';\n            }\n\n            async processInput(input) {\n                if (!input.trim()) return;\n\n                this.addOutput(\'I\', `User: ${input}`, 1.00);\n                this.updateMetrics();\n\n                if (input.startsWith(\'/\')) {\n                    this.processCommand(input);\n                } else {\n                    this.processNaturalLanguage(input);\n                }\n            }\n\n            processCommand(cmd) {\n                const parts = cmd.split(\' \');\n                const command = parts[0].toLowerCase();\n\n                switch(command) {\n                    case \'/demo\':\n                        this.runDemo(parts[1] || \'confidence_gating\');\n                        break;\n                    case \'/spec\':\n                        this.generateSpec(parts[1] || \'auth\');\n                        break;\n                    case \'/help\':\n                        this.showHelp();\n                        break;\n                    default:\n                        this.addOutput(\'E\', `Unknown command: ${command}`, 0.00);\n                }\n            }\n\n            async processNaturalLanguage(query) {\n                this.addOutput(\'I\', \'Consulting multi-LLM system...\', 0.85);\n                \n                await this.sleep(800);\n                this.addOutput(\'I\', \'Groq: Fast inference complete\', 0.92);\n                \n with high confidence`, 0.96);\n            }\n\n            async runDemo(demoType) {\n                this.addOutput(\'S\', `Starting demo: ${demoType}`, 1.00);\n\n                switch(demoType) {\n                    case \'confidence_gating\':\n                        await this.demoConfidenceGating();\n                        break;\n                    case \'expert_disagreement\':\n = false;\n                this.currentPhase = \'idle\';\n                this.pendingApproval = null;\n                \n                this.setupEventListeners();\n            }\n\n            setupEventListeners() {\n                this.terminalInput.addEventListener(\'keypress\', (e) => {\n                    if (e.key === \'Enter\') {\n                        this.processCommand(this.terminalInput.value);\n                        this.terminalInput.value = \'\';\n                    }\n                });\n\n                document.getElementById(\'approveBtn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n                    this.handleApproval(true);\n                });\n\n                document.getElementById(\'rejectBtn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n                    this.handleApproval(false);\n                });\n            }\n\n            addOutput(tag, message, confidence = null) {\n                const line = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                line.className = \'output-line\';\n                \n                const tagSpan = document.createElement(\'span\');\n                tagSpan.className = `tag tag-${tag.toLowerCase()}`;\n                tagSpan.textContent = tag.toUpperCase();\n                \n                const messageSpan = document.createElement(\'span\');\n                messageSpan.textContent = message;\n                \n                line.appendChild(tagSpan);\n                line.appendChild(messageSpan);\n                \n                if (confidence !== null) {\n                    const confSpan = document.createElement(\'span\');\n                    confSpan.className = `confidence ${this.getConfidenceClass(confidence)}`;\n                    confSpan.textContent = confidence.toFixed(2);\n                    line.appendChild(confSpan);\n                }\n                \n                this.terminalOutput.appendChild(line);\n                this.terminalOutput.scrollTop = this.terminalOutput.scrollHeight;\n            }\n\n            getConfidenceClass(conf) {\n                if (conf >= 0.8) return \'conf-high\';\n                if (conf >= 0.5) return \'conf-medium\';\n                return \'conf-low\';\n            }\n\n            updateMetrics() {\n                document.getElementById(\'loopsComplete\').textContent = this.loopsCompleted;\n                document.getElementById(\'gatesActive\').textContent = this.gatesActive;\n                document.getElementById(\'testsPassed\').textContent = this.testsPassed;\n                document.getElementById(\'automationsRunning\').textContent = this.automationsRunning;\n                document.getElementById(\'humanApprovals\').textContent = this.humanApprovals;\n            }\n\n            updateLoopProgress(loopIndex, phase, progress) {\n                const loop = document.querySelector(`[data-loop="${loopIndex}"]`);\n                if (loop) {\n                    loop.classList.add(\'active\');\n                    loop.querySelector(\'.loop-progress\').textContent = phase;\n                    loop.querySelector(\'.progress-fill\').style.width = progress + \'%\';\n                    \n                    if (progress >= 100) {\n                        loop.classList.remove(\'active\');\n                        loop.classList.add(\'complete\');\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n container.appendChild(gate);\n                this.gatesActive++;\n                this.updateMetrics();\n            }\n\n            async processCommand(cmd) {\n                const command = cmd.trim().toLowerCase();\n                \n                this.addOutput(\'info\', `> ${cmd}`, null);\n                \n                if (command === \'start\') {\n                    await this.startSystem();\n                } else if (command === \'help\') {\n                    this.showHelp();\n                } else if (command === \'status\') {\n                    this.showStatus();\n                } else if (command === \'reset\') {\n                    location.reload();\n                } else {\n                    this.addOutput(\'info\', \'Unknown command. Type "help" for available commands.\', null);\n                }\n            }\n\n            showHelp() {\n                this.addOutput(\'info\', \'Available commands:\', null);\n this.addOutput(\'info\', \'  reset  - Reset the system\', null);\n                this.addOutput(\'info\', \'  help   - Show this help message\', null);\n            }\n\n            showStatus() {\n async startSystem() {\n                if (this.isRunning) {\n                    this.addOutput(\'info\', \'System is already running\', null);\n                    return;\n                }\n                 line.appendChild(confSpan);\n                }\n                \n                this.terminalOutput.appendChild(line);\n                this.terminalOutput.scrollTop = this.terminalOutput.scrollHeight;\n            }\n\n            getConfidenceClass(conf) {\n                if (conf >= 0.8) return \'conf-high\';\n                if (conf >= 0.5) return \'conf-medium\';\n                return \'conf-low\';\n            }\n\n            updateMetrics() {\n                document.getElementById(\'loopsComplete\').textContent = this.loopsCompleted;\n             const command = cmd.trim().toLowerCase();\n                \n                this.addOutput(\'info\', `> ${cmd}`, null);\n                \n                if (command === \'start\') {\n        this.showStatus();\n                } else if (command === \'reset\') {\n                    location.reload();\n                } else {\n                    this.addOutput(\'info\', \'Unknown this.addOutput(\'info\', \'  reset  - Reset the system\', null);\n                this.addOutput(\'info\', \'  help   - Show this help message\', null);\n            }\n\n            showStatus() {\n async startSystem() {\n                if (this.isRunning) {\n                    this.addOutput(\'info\', \'System is already running\', null);\n                    return;\n                }\n <!-- Terminal Area -->\n        <div class="terminal-area">\n            <div class="terminal-header">\n                <span id="terminalTitle">SYSTEM TERMINAL</span>\n                <div                 <button class="action-btn" id="clearBtn">CLEAR</button>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n            \n            <div class="terminal-output" id="terminalOutput">\n                <div class="output-line">\n                    <span class="tag tag-system">SYSTEM</span>\n                    <span>Murphy Integrated System initialized</span>\n                    <span class="confidence conf-high">1.00</span>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="terminal-input-area">\n                <span class="prompt">murphy></span>\n                <input type="text" class="terminal-input" id="terminalInput" placeholder="Enter command...">\n            </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <!-- Sidebar -->\n        <div class="sidebar">\n            <div class="sidebar-section">\n                <div class="sidebar-title">📊 System Metrics</div>\n                <div class="metric-item">\n                    <span class="metric-label">States Generated</span>\n                    <span class="metric-value" id="statesGenerated">0</span>\n                </div>\n                <div class="metric-item">\n                    <span class="metric-label">Artifacts Created</span>\n                    <span class="metric-value" id="artifactsCreated">0</span>\n                </div>\n                <div class="metric-item">\n                    <span class="metric-label">Gates Active</span>\n                    <span class="metric-value" id="gatesActive">0</span>\n                </div>\n                <div class="metric-item">\n                    <span class="metric-label">Swarms Running</span>\n                    <span class="metric-value" id="swarmsRunning">0</span>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="sidebar-section">\n                <div class="sidebar-title">🐝 Active Swarms</div>\n                <div id="swarmsContainer">\n                    <div style="color: #666; font-size: 10px; padding: 8px;">No swarms active</div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="sidebar-section">\n                <div class="sidebar-title">📦 Generated Artifacts</div>\n                <div id="artifactsContainer">\n                    <div style="color: #666; font-size: 10px; padding: 8px;">No artifacts yet</div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n\n    <!-- Detail Modal -->\n    <div class="modal-overlay" id="modalOverlay"></div>\n    <div class="detail-modal" id="detailModal">\n        <div class="modal-header" id="modalHeader"></div>\n        <div class="modal-content" id="modalContent"></div>\n        <div class="button-group">\n            <button class="btn" id="evolveBtn">EVOLVE STATE</button>\n            <button class="btn" id="regenerateModalBtn">REGENERATE</button>\n            <button class="btn btn-danger" id="closeModalBtn">CLOSE</button>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n\n    <script>\n        class MurphyIntegratedSystem {\n            constructor() {\n                this.terminalOutput = document.getElementById(\'terminalOutput\');\n                this.terminalInput = document.getElementById(\'terminalInput\');\n                this.stateTreeContainer = document.getElementById(\'stateTreeContainer\');\n                this.swarmsContainer = document.getElementById(\'swarmsContainer\');\n                this.artifactsContainer = document.getElementById(\'artifactsContainer\');\n                \n                this.states = [];\n                this.currentState = null;\n                this.artifacts = [];\n                this.swarms = [];\n                this.stateIdCounter = 0;\n                \n                this.metrics = {\n                    statesGenerated: 0,\n                    artifactsCreated: 0,\n                    gatesActive: 0,\n                    swarmsRunning: 0\n                };\n                \n                this.llmStatus = {\n                    groq: \'standby\',\n                    aristotle: \'standby\',\n                    onboard: \'standby\'\n                };\n                \n                this.setupEventListeners();\n            }\n\n            setupEventListeners() {\n                document.getElementById(\'startButton\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n                    this.initialize();\n                });\n\n                this.terminalInput.addEventListener(\'keypress\', (e) => {\n                    if (e.key === \'Enter\') {\n                        this.processCommand(this.terminalInput.value);\n                        this.terminalInput.value = \'\';\n                    }\n                });\n\n                document.getElementById(\'regenerateBtn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n                    if (this.currentState) this.regenerateState(this.currentState);\n                });\n\n                document.getElementById(\'rollbackBtn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n                    this.rollbackState();\n                });\n\n                document.getElementById(\'clearBtn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n                    this.terminalOutput.innerHTML = \'\';\n                });\n\n                document.getElementById(\'closeModalBtn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n                    this.closeModal();\n                });\n\n                document.getElementById(\'evolveBtn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n                    if (this.currentState) this.evolveState(this.currentState);\n                });\n\n                document.getElementById(\'regenerateModalBtn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n                    if (this.currentState) {\n                        this.regenerateState(this.currentState);\n                        this.closeModal();\n                    }\n                });\n            }\n\n            async initialize() {\n                document.getElementById(\'startOverlay\').style.display = \'none\';\n                \n                this.addOutput(\'system\', \'Initializing Murphy Integrated System...\', 1.00);\n                await this.sleep(500);\n                \n                // Initialize LLMs\n                await this.initializeLLMs();\n                \n                // Create root state\n                await this.createRootState();\n                \n                this.addOutput(\'success\', \'System ready. Type "help" for commands.\', 1.00);\n            }\n\n            async initializeLLMs() {\n                this.addOutput(\'llm\', \'Initializing LLM providers...\', 0.95);\n                await this.sleep(800);\n                \n                // Groq\n                this.setLLMStatus(\'groq\', \'active\');\n                this.addOutput(\'llm\', \'Groq LLM: Active (Fast Inference)\', 0.98);\n                await this.sleep(500);\n                \n                // Aristotle\n                this.setLLMStatus(\'aristotle\', \'active\');\n                this.addOutput(\'llm\', \'Aristotle LLM: Active (Reasoning)\', 0.96);\n                await this.sleep(500);\n                \n                // Onboard\n                this.setLLMStatus(\'onboard\', \'active\');\n                this.addOutput(\'llm\', \'Onboard LLM: Active (Fallback)\', 0.94);\n                await this.sleep(500);\n            }\n\n            setLLMStatus(llm, status) {\n                this.llmStatus[llm] = status;\n                const indicator = document.getElementById(`${llm}Indicator`);\n                const dot = indicator.querySelector(\'.llm-dot\');\n                dot.className = `llm-dot llm-${status}`;\n            }\n\n            async createRootState() {\n                const rootState = {\n                    id: this.stateIdCounter++,\n                    title: \'Business System Root\',\n                    type: \'root\',\n                    confidence: 1.00,\n                    parent: null,\n                    children: [],\n                    data: {\n                        description: \'Root state for business management system\',\n                        components: [\'Executive\', \'Marketing\', \'Sales\', \'Operations\', \'Finance\'],\n                        status: \'initialized\'\n                    }\n                };\n                \n                this.states.push(rootState);\n                this.currentState = rootState;\n                this.metrics.statesGenerated++;\n                this.updateMetrics();\n                \n                this.renderStateTree();\n                this.addOutput(\'state\', `Created root state: ${rootState.title}`, rootState.confidence);\n                \n                // Auto-generate initial children\n                await this.sleep(1000);\n                await this.generateInitialStates(rootState);\n            }\n\n            async generateInitialStates(parentState) {\n                this.addOutput(\'swarm\', \'Activating swarm generation for initial states...\', 0.92);\n                \n                const swarmTypes = [\'CREATIVE\', \'ANALYTICAL\', \'HYBRID\'];\n                const initialStates = [\n                    { title: \'Executive Dashboard\', type: \'component\', swarm: \'ANALYTICAL\' },\n                    { title: \'Marketing System\', type: \'component\', swarm: \'CREATIVE\' },\n                    { title: \'Sales Pipeline\', type: \'component\', swarm: \'HYBRID\' },\n                    { title: \'Operations Manager\', type: \'component\', swarm: \'ANALYTICAL\' },\n                    { title: \'Financial Tracking\', type: \'component\', swarm: \'ANALYTICAL\' }\n                ];\n                \n                for (const stateConfig of initialStates) {\n                    await this.sleep(600);\n                    const newState = await this.createChildState(parentState, stateConfig);\n                    this.activateSwarm(stateConfig.swarm, newState);\n                }\n                \n                this.addOutput(\'success\', \'Initial state generation complete\', 0.95);\n            }\n\n            async createChildState(parentState, config) {\n                const childState = {\n                    id: this.stateIdCounter++,\n                    title: config.title,\n                    type: config.type,\n                    confidence: 0.85 + Math.random() * 0.10,\n                    parent: parentState.id,\n                    children: [],\n                    data: {\n                        description: `Generated ${config.type}: ${config.title}`,\n                        swarmType: config.swarm,\n                        status: \'active\',\n                        artifacts: []\n                    }\n                };\n                \n                this.states.push(childState);\n                parentState.children.push(childState.id);\n                this.metrics.statesGenerated++;\n                this.updateMetrics();\n                \n                this.renderStateTree();\n                this.addOutput(\'state\', `Generated child state: ${childState.title}`, childState.confidence);\n                \n                return childState;\n            }\n\n            activateSwarm(type, state) {\n                const swarm = {\n                    id: `swarm-${this.swarms.length}`,\n                    type: type,\n                    stateId: state.id,\n                    status: \'active\',\n                    progress: 0\n                };\n                \n                this.swarms.push(swarm);\n                this.metrics.swarmsRunning++;\n                this.updateMetrics();\n                this.renderSwarms();\n                \n                this.addOutput(\'swarm\', `Activated ${type} swarm for ${state.title}`, 0.90);\n                \n                // Simulate swarm progress\n                this.simulateSwarmProgress(swarm, state);\n            }\n\n            async simulateSwarmProgress(swarm, state) {\n                for (let i = 0; i < 5; i++) {\n                    await this.sleep(1000);\n                    swarm.progress += 20;\n                    this.renderSwarms();\n                    \n                    if (swarm.progress >= 100) {\n                        this.generateArtifact(state, swarm.type);\n                        swarm.status = \'complete\';\n                        this.metrics.swarmsRunning--;\n                        this.updateMetrics();\n                        this.renderSwarms();\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            generateArtifact(state, swarmType) {\n                const artifact = {\n                    id: `artifact-${this.artifacts.length}`,\n                    title: `${state.title} Specification`,\n                    stateId: state.id,\n                    swarmType: swarmType,\n                    confidence: 0.88 + Math.random() * 0.10,\n                    data: {\n                        type: \'specification\',\n                        content: `Generated by ${swarmType} swarm`,\n                        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n                    }\n                };\n                \n                this.artifacts.push(artifact);\n                state.data.artifacts.push(artifact.id);\n                this.metrics.artifactsCreated++;\n                this.updateMetrics();\n                this.renderArtifacts();\n                \n                this.addOutput(\'success\', `Generated artifact: ${artifact.title}`, artifact.confidence);\n            }\n\n            renderStateTree() {\n                this.stateTreeContainer.innerHTML = \'\';\n                \n                const rootStates = this.states.filter(s => s.parent === null);\n                rootStates.forEach(state => {\n                    this.renderStateNode(state, 0);\n                });\n            }\n\n            renderStateNode(state, depth) {\n                const node = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                node.className = \'state-node\' + (depth > 0 ? \' child\' : \'\');\n                if (this.currentState && this.currentState.id === state.id) {\n                    node.classList.add(\'active\');\n                }\n                \n                node.innerHTML = `\n                    <div class="node-title">${state.title}</div>\n                    <div class="node-status">${state.type} • ${state.data.status}</div>\n                    <div class="node-confidence">${state.confidence.toFixed(2)}</div>\n                `;\n                \n                node.addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n                    this.selectState(state);\n                });\n                \n                this.stateTreeContainer.appendChild(node);\n                \n                // Render children\n                state.children.forEach(childId => {\n                    const childState = this.states.find(s => s.id === childId);\n                    if (childState) {\n                        this.renderStateNode(childState, depth + 1);\n                    }\n                });\n            }\n\n            selectState(state) {\n                this.currentState = state;\n                this.renderStateTree();\n                \n                // Show state details in terminal\n                this.terminalOutput.innerHTML = \'\';\n                this.addOutput(\'state\', `Selected: ${state.title}`, state.confidence);\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', `Type: ${state.type}`, null);\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', `Status: ${state.data.status}`, null);\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', `Artifacts: ${state.data.artifacts.length}`, null);\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', `Children: ${state.children.length}`, null);\n                \n                // Show detailed modal\n                this.showStateDetails(state);\n            }\n\n            showStateDetails(state) {\n                document.getElementById(\'modalHeader\').textContent = state.title;\n                \n                let content = `\n                    <div class="modal-section">\n                        <div class="section-header">State Information</div>\n                        <div>ID: ${state.id}</div>\n                        <div>Type: ${state.type}</div>\n                        <div>Confidence: ${state.confidence.toFixed(2)}</div>\n                        <div>Status: ${state.data.status}</div>\n                    </div>\n                    \n                    <div class="modal-section">\n                        <div class="section-header">Description</div>\n                        <div>${state.data.description}</div>\n                    </div>\n                    \n                    <div class="modal-section">\n                        <div class="section-header">Swarm Type</div>\n                        <div>${state.data.swarmType || \'None\'}</div>\n                    </div>\n                    \n                    <div class="modal-section">\n                        <div class="section-header">Artifacts (${state.data.artifacts.length})</div>\n                `;\n                \n                state.data.artifacts.forEach(artifactId => {\n                    const artifact = this.artifacts.find(a => a.id === artifactId);\n                    if (artifact) {\n                        content += `<div>• ${artifact.title} (${artifact.confidence.toFixed(2)})</div>`;\n                    }\n                });\n                \n                content += `\n                    </div>\n                    \n                    <div class="modal-section">\n                        <div class="section-header">Child States (${state.children.length})</div>\n                `;\n                \n                state.children.forEach(childId => {\n                    const child = this.states.find(s => s.id === childId);\n                    if (child) {\n                        content += `<div>• ${child.title}</div>`;\n                    }\n                });\n                \n                content += `</div>`;\n                \n                document.getElementById(\'modalContent\').innerHTML = content;\n                document.getElementById(\'modalOverlay\').classList.add(\'active\');\n                document.getElementById(\'detailModal\').classList.add(\'active\');\n            }\n\n            closeModal() {\n                document.getElementById(\'modalOverlay\').classList.remove(\'active\');\n                document.getElementById(\'detailModal\').classList.remove(\'active\');\n            }\n\n            async evolveState(state) {\n                this.closeModal();\n                this.addOutput(\'state\', `Evolving state: ${state.title}...`, 0.90);\n                \n                await this.sleep(800);\n                \n                const childConfig = {\n                    title: `${state.title} - Enhanced`,\n                    type: \'evolution\',\n                    swarm: \'HYBRID\'\n                };\n                \n                const newState = await this.createChildState(state, childConfig);\n                this.activateSwarm(\'HYBRID\', newState);\n                \n                this.addOutput(\'success\', `State evolved successfully`, 0.92);\n            }\n\n            async regenerateState(state) {\n                this.addOutput(\'state\', `Regenerating state: ${state.title}...`, 0.88);\n                \n                await this.sleep(1000);\n                \n                state.confidence = 0.85 + Math.random() * 0.12;\n                state.data.status = \'regenerated\';\n                \n                this.renderStateTree();\n                this.addOutput(\'success\', `State regenerated with confidence ${state.confidence.toFixed(2)}`, state.confidence);\n            }\n\n            rollbackState() {\n                if (!this.currentState || !this.currentState.parent) {\n                    this.addOutput(\'error\', \'Cannot rollback root state\', 0.00);\n                    return;\n                }\n                \n                const parentState = this.states.find(s => s.id === this.currentState.parent);\n                if (parentState) {\n                    this.selectState(parentState);\n                    this.addOutput(\'state\', `Rolled back to: ${parentState.title}`, parentState.confidence);\n                }\n            }\n\n            renderSwarms() {\n                if (this.swarms.length === 0) {\n                    this.swarmsContainer.innerHTML = \'<div style="color: #666; font-size: 10px; padding: 8px;">No swarms active</div>\';\n                    return;\n                }\n                \n                this.swarmsContainer.innerHTML = \'\';\n                this.swarms.filter(s => s.status === \'active\').forEach(swarm => {\n                    const state = this.states.find(s => s.id === swarm.stateId);\n                    const div = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                    div.className = \'swarm-status\';\n                    div.innerHTML = `\n                        <div class="swarm-type">${swarm.type}</div>\n                        <div class="swarm-info">${state ? state.title : \'Unknown\'}</div>\n                        <div class="swarm-info">Progress: ${swarm.progress}%</div>\n                    `;\n                    this.swarmsContainer.appendChild(div);\n                });\n            }\n\n            renderArtifacts() {\n                if (this.artifacts.length === 0) {\n                    this.artifactsContainer.innerHTML = \'<div style="color: #666; font-size: 10px; padding: 8px;">No artifacts yet</div>\';\n                    return;\n                }\n                \n                this.artifactsContainer.innerHTML = \'\';\n                this.artifacts.slice(-5).reverse().forEach(artifact => {\n                    const div = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                    div.className = \'artifact-box\';\n                    div.innerHTML = `\n                        <div class="artifact-title">${artifact.title}</div>\n                        <div class="artifact-stats">Confidence: ${artifact.confidence.toFixed(2)} • ${artifact.swarmType}</div>\n                    `;\n                    div.addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n                        this.showArtifactDetails(artifact);\n                    });\n                    this.artifactsContainer.appendChild(div);\n                });\n            }\n\n            showArtifactDetails(artifact) {\n                const state = this.states.find(s => s.id === artifact.stateId);\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', `Artifact: ${artifact.title}`, artifact.confidence);\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', `State: ${state ? state.title : \'Unknown\'}`, null);\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', `Swarm: ${artifact.swarmType}`, null);\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', `Type: ${artifact.data.type}`, null);\n            }\n\n            processCommand(cmd) {\n                const command = cmd.trim().toLowerCase();\n                \n                this.addOutput(\'system\', `> ${cmd}`, null);\n                \n                if (command === \'help\') {\n                    this.showHelp();\n                } else if (command === \'status\') {\n                    this.showStatus();\n                } else if (command.startsWith(\'evolve\')) {\n                    if (this.currentState) {\n                        this.evolveState(this.currentState);\n                    }\n                } else if (command.startsWith(\'regenerate\')) {\n                    if (this.currentState) {\n                        this.regenerateState(this.currentState);\n                    }\n                } else if (command === \'rollback\') {\n                    this.rollbackState();\n                } else {\n                    this.addOutput(\'error\', \'Unknown command. Type "help" for available commands.\', 0.00);\n                }\n            }\n\n            showHelp() {\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', \'Available commands:\', null);\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', \'  help       - Show this help\', null);\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', \'  status     - Show system status\', null);\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', \'  evolve     - Evolve current state\', null);\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', \'  regenerate - Regenerate current state\', null);\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', \'  rollback   - Rollback to parent state\', null);\n            }\n\n            showStatus() {\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', \'=== SYSTEM STATUS ===\', null);\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', `States: ${this.metrics.statesGenerated}`, null);\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', `Artifacts: ${this.metrics.artifactsCreated}`, null);\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', `Active Swarms: ${this.metrics.swarmsRunning}`, null);\n                this.addOutput(\'system\', `Current State: ${this.currentState ? this.currentState.title : \'None\'}`, null);\n            }\n\n            addOutput(tag, message, confidence = null) {\n                const line = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                line.className = \'output-line\';\n                \n                const tagSpan = document.createElement(\'span\');\n                tagSpan.className = `tag tag-${tag}`;\n                tagSpan.textContent = tag.toUpperCase();\n                \n                const messageSpan = document.createElement(\'span\');\n                messageSpan.textContent = message;\n                \n                line.appendChild(tagSpan);\n                line.appendChild(messageSpan);\n                \n                if (confidence !== null) {\n                    const confSpan = document.createElement(\'span\');\n                    confSpan.className = `confidence ${this.getConfidenceClass(confidence)}`;\n                    confSpan.textContent = confidence.toFixed(2);\n                    line.appendChild(confSpan);\n                }\n                \n                this.terminalOutput.appendChild(line);\n                this.terminalOutput.scrollTop = this.terminalOutput.scrollHeight;\n            }\n\n            getConfidenceClass(conf) {\n                if (conf >= 0.8) return \'conf-high\';\n                if (conf >= 0.5) return \'conf-medium\';\n                return \'conf-low\';\n            }\n\n            updateMetrics() {\n                document.getElementById(\'statesGenerated\').textContent = this.metrics.statesGenerated;\n                document.getElementById(\'artifactsCreated\').textContent = this.metrics.artifactsCreated;\n                document.getElementById(\'gatesActive\').textContent = this.metrics.gatesActive;\n                document.getElementById(\'swarmsRunning\').textContent = this.metrics.swarmsRunning;\n            }\n\n            sleep(ms) {\n                return new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Initialize Murphy Integrated System\n        const murphy = new MurphyIntegratedSystem();\n    </script>\n</body>\n</html>\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}
